6th September 2014.I would be grateful if you could circulate the Call for Papers (attached) whi=
ch is also available at http://hridigital.shef.ac.uk/dhc2014We are delighted to announce that our three Keynote Speakers will be:Professor Laura Mandell (Director, Initiative for Digital Humanities, Media a=
nd Culture, Texas A & M University).Dr Fred Truyen (Associate Professor in the Faculty of Arts and Head of CS/Dig=
ital Media Lab at the Institute for  Cultural Studies, KU Leuven).Professor Paul Arthur (Professor of Digital Humanities, The University of Wes=
tern Sydney).With best wishes
Mike--=20
